# ATtiny13A_Serial_CoMCU

## Serial Protocol

```
> "C:1\n"
< "@=@@W\n"
> "4:1122334455cscs\n"
> "3:1122334455cscs\n"
> "2:1122334455cscs\n"
> "1:1122334455cscs\n"
```
